@@ -96,6 +96,22 @@ function createWindow () {
 	// Create the browser window.
 	mainWindow = new BrowserWindow(electronOptions);
 
+	mainWindow.webContents.session.setPermissionRequestHandler((webContents, permission, callback) => {
+		const cameraPermissions = new Set(["media", "camera", "microphone"]);
+		if (!cameraPermissions.has(permission)) {
+			callback(false);
+			return;
+		}
+
+		try {
+			const requestUrl = new URL(webContents.getURL());
+			const isLocalhost = ["localhost", "127.0.0.1", "::1", "::ffff:127.0.0.1"].includes(requestUrl.hostname);
+			callback(isLocalhost);
+		} catch {
+			callback(false);
+		}
+	});
+

 	 * If config.address is not defined or is an empty string (listening on all interfaces), connect to localhost
